Non Stop Blackjack 21 fun is here!\r\nBlackjack is also know as 21 or twenty-one is a widely played casino banking game. \r\n\r\nBlackjack 21 is a comparing card game between a player and a dealer, meaning players will compete against a dealer but not against other players and is played with one or more decks of 52 cards. \r\n\r\nA Blackjack 21 game can be won in the following ways:\r\n\r\n✔ Getting 21 points on the player's first 2 cards which is called a 'blackjack', 'natural' assuming the dealer has not got a blackjack\r\n✔ Get a score higher than the dealer without exceeding 21\r\n✔ Allowing the dealer to draw additional cards until his hand exceeds 21\r\n\r\nWhen the game of blackjack 21 starts the player or players are dealt with a two card hand and add together the value of their cards. The Face cards which are kings, queens and jacks are counted as 10 points. The dealer and the player count an ace as 1 point or 11 points, and all other cards are counted according to the numeric value shown on the card. The players after receiving their first two cards, have an option of getting a hit or taking an additional card. CallBreak is also known as Lakdi/Lakadi in India.\r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to score the highest points of all as well as to stop other players from getting higher points by breaking their call (Hence the name \"CallBreak\").\r\n\r\nThis game is normally played using a standard 52-card pack. The cards of each suit rank from high to low A-K-Q-J-10-9-8-7-6-5-4-3-2. Spades are permanent trumps: any card of the Spade suit beats any card of any other suit.\r\n\r\nCallBreak Multiplayer is a strategic trick-based card game. Deal and play are counter-clockwise. To succeed, a player must win the number of tricks called, or more trick than the call. If a player succeeds, the number called is added to his or her cumulative score. Otherwise the number called is subtracted. After the end of fifth round the winner is decided, player with higher total points is considered as the winner of the game.\r\n\r\nCallBreak is a famous Nepali brain teasing trick card game which is wildly popular.\r\n\r\nThe best part about the CallBreak Multiplayer is being able to connect with your friends an play for hours at a stretch.\r\n\r\nWhy don't you try it right now? \r\n\r\nDownload CallBreak Multiplayer today for free and you'll find an easy way to spend your time with excellent emotions!\r\n\r\nTry it and nourish your card skills !!\r\n\r\n◆◆◆◆ CallBreak Multiplayer Features ◆◆◆◆\r\n\r\n✓ Very fun and easy to play\r\n✓ Extreme User Friendly: Easy and refreshing interface\r\n✓ Compatible for both ARM and x86 devices.\r\n\r\nPlease don't forget to Rate and Review CallBreak Multiplayer, we aim to make Call \r\nBreak one of the best card games out there on the Windows Store.\r\n\r\nWe will be grateful to hear your opinions and improve - whenever needed - in future versions.\r\n\r\nEnjoy playing CallBreak Multiplayer!!","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"},{"$type":"Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts.V8.One.CardModel, Microsoft.Marketplace.Storefront.Contracts","ProductId":"9NZG3BQPGKJ2","TileLayout":"Square","Title":"Kahoot!
